>
> **[2:20](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/real-world-gis-22715766/how-can-you-master-the-gis-job-interview-part-1?u=76281980&t=140)** Look at its websites and social media presence.
>
> **[2:24](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/real-world-gis-22715766/how-can-you-master-the-gis-job-interview-part-1?u=76281980&t=144)** Be able to articulate also why you're interested in working at that company, and connect it to their mission in the interview process.
>
> **[2:34](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/real-world-gis-22715766/how-can-you-master-the-gis-job-interview-part-1?u=76281980&t=154)** And if you don't understand something, ask for clarification.

#### How can you master the GIS job interview? Part 2
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/real-world-gis-22715766/how-can-you-master-the-gis-job-interview-part-2?u=76281980)

> [!transcript]- Transcript
>
> **[0:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/real-world-gis-22715766/how-can-you-master-the-gis-job-interview-part-2?u=76281980&t=0)** - [Narrator] Now let's take a look at the specifics for the GIS job interview.
>
> **[0:06](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/real-world-gis-22715766/how-can-you-master-the-gis-job-interview-part-2?u=76281980&t=6)** You should prepare and review what you know and be ready to summarize what you've done in GIS.
>
> **[0:13](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/real-world-gis-22715766/how-can-you-master-the-gis-job-interview-part-2?u=76281980&t=13)** They have your resume, so that is what they'll be working off of most likely unless they've asked you to submit other details like a portfolio or answers to questions.
>
> **[0:23](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/real-world-gis-22715766/how-can-you-master-the-gis-job-interview-part-2?u=76281980&t=23)** If you don't have a portfolio all ready to go, you should get one together.
>
> **[0:28](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/real-world-gis-22715766/how-can-you-master-the-gis-job-interview-part-2?u=76281980&t=28)** I have mine in both a digital and a paper form.
>
> **[0:31](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/real-world-gis-22715766/how-can-you-master-the-gis-job-interview-part-2?u=76281980&t=31)** Make it look organized and clear, however, and put it together beforehand.
>
> **[0:37](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/real-world-gis-22715766/how-can-you-master-the-gis-job-interview-part-2?u=76281980&t=37)** Try to be specific and point out in that process the projects that you've worked on.
>
> **[0:43](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/real-world-gis-22715766/how-can-you-master-the-gis-job-interview-part-2?u=76281980&t=43)** Now, you should try and write down questions that you would ask about GIS if you were the one hiring in their place and then try to answer them.
>
> **[0:54](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/real-world-gis-22715766/how-can-you-master-the-gis-job-interview-part-2?u=76281980&t=54)** Anticipate the interview questions as best you can.
>
> **[0:58](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/real-world-gis-22715766/how-can-you-master-the-gis-job-interview-part-2?u=76281980&t=58)** You should be ready to articulate your GIS skills in about a minute.
>
> **[1:02](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/real-world-gis-22715766/how-can-you-master-the-gis-job-interview-part-2?u=76281980&t=62)** I know this is hard, but do it.
>
> **[1:04](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/real-world-gis-22715766/how-can-you-master-the-gis-job-interview-part-2?u=76281980&t=64)** Practice it, because they will ask for them.
>
> **[1:07](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/real-world-gis-22715766/how-can-you-master-the-gis-job-interview-part-2?u=76281980&t=67)** Your resume will say what GIS software you are trained in, but you should be ready to let them know what you can use, including the extensions you know if you know them, like Business Analyst or Network Analyst, for example, in the Esri software.
>
> **[1:22](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/real-world-gis-22715766/how-can-you-master-the-gis-job-interview-part-2?u=76281980&t=82)** Also, you should be able to describe the projects and the training that you've had and be prepared to show them an online demonstration or a paper map or report of your work.
>
> **[1:32](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/real-world-gis-22715766/how-can-you-master-the-gis-job-interview-part-2?u=76281980&t=92)** Now don't force it in the interview, but be ready to show them what you've done if they ask.
>
> **[1:37](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/real-world-gis-22715766/how-can-you-master-the-gis-job-interview-part-2?u=76281980&t=97)** Proving the success of your work goes a long way.
>
> **[1:41](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/real-world-gis-22715766/how-can-you-master-the-gis-job-interview-part-2?u=76281980&t=101)** If the company is using a certain GIS data set, you should learn it.
>
> **[1:46](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/real-world-gis-22715766/how-can-you-master-the-gis-job-interview-part-2?u=76281980&t=106)** If they ask about something like OpenStreetMap or you know that they're using a specific kind of GPS unit, then you should learn about that if you don't know about it.
>
> **[1:56](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/real-world-gis-22715766/how-can-you-master-the-gis-job-interview-part-2?u=76281980&t=116)** Don't come into the interview without that knowledge.
>
> **[1:59](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/real-world-gis-22715766/how-can-you-master-the-gis-job-interview-part-2?u=76281980&t=119)** Check on their website to see these kinds of details.
>
> **[2:03](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/real-world-gis-22715766/how-can-you-master-the-gis-job-interview-part-2?u=76281980&t=123)** Do your homework to win this job.
>
> **[2:06](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/real-world-gis-22715766/how-can-you-master-the-gis-job-interview-part-2?u=76281980&t=126)** Also, you should be able to describe your programming skills but friends, do this honestly.
>
> **[2:13](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/real-world-gis-22715766/how-can-you-master-the-gis-job-interview-part-2?u=76281980&t=133)** They might challenge you on it.
>
> **[2:15](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/real-world-gis-22715766/how-can-you-master-the-gis-job-interview-part-2?u=76281980&t=135)** If you have no experience, then start getting some by watching courses on [linkedin.com](https://linkedin.com) for programming languages that the GIS industry uses, for example.
>
> **[2:26](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/real-world-gis-22715766/how-can-you-master-the-gis-job-interview-part-2?u=76281980&t=146)** In the Esri software, it's primarily using Python for scripting, but if you don't actually know Python, then don't say that you do.
>
> **[2:35](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/real-world-gis-22715766/how-can-you-master-the-gis-job-interview-part-2?u=76281980&t=155)** We teach Python and Python scripting and GIS at my university and there's a clear difference.
>
> **[2:41](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/real-world-gis-22715766/how-can-you-master-the-gis-job-interview-part-2?u=76281980&t=161)** Python is a full programming language while Python scripting and GIS is using Python code to run GID toolbox operations.
>
> **[2:50](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/real-world-gis-22715766/how-can-you-master-the-gis-job-interview-part-2?u=76281980&t=170)** If the company needs someone who can code in Python, then be specific about what you know.
>
> **[2:57](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/real-world-gis-22715766/how-can-you-master-the-gis-job-interview-part-2?u=76281980&t=177)** Honesty truly is the best policy and be ready to state what you think you can deliver in the form of GIS skills to the company.
>
> **[3:06](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/real-world-gis-22715766/how-can-you-master-the-gis-job-interview-part-2?u=76281980&t=186)** Be able to give them answers about your timeliness on completion of projects and general approaches to GIS work.
>
> **[3:13](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/real-world-gis-22715766/how-can-you-master-the-gis-job-interview-part-2?u=76281980&t=193)** I encourage my students to remember these three P's, you bring a positive attitude, you have patience teaching troubleshooting for others, and GIS has power to transform their business.
>
> **[3:27](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/real-world-gis-22715766/how-can-you-master-the-gis-job-interview-part-2?u=76281980&t=207)** Positive attitude, patience, and power, those are compelling to a business.
>
> **[3:32](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/real-world-gis-22715766/how-can-you-master-the-gis-job-interview-part-2?u=76281980&t=212)** And try to anticipate questions about how GIS will benefit the company even more.
>
> **[3:39](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/real-world-gis-22715766/how-can-you-master-the-gis-job-interview-part-2?u=76281980&t=219)** It's a good idea to think about how to describe the ways you continue to learn about GIS and how you interact with the GIS community to learn more.
>
> **[3:50](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/real-world-gis-22715766/how-can-you-master-the-gis-job-interview-part-2?u=76281980&t=230)** Seriously, this gives potential employers confidence about your continuing education in GIS and how it'll benefit the company.
>
> **[3:58](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/real-world-gis-22715766/how-can-you-master-the-gis-job-interview-part-2?u=76281980&t=238)** You know that GIS software is always changing, so you should be able to say in the interview how you handle learning something that's always changing.
>
> **[4:08](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/real-world-gis-22715766/how-can-you-master-the-gis-job-interview-part-2?u=76281980&t=248)** Lastly, you need to tell them how these projects that you've completed have been done independently or successfully in group environments.
>
> **[4:17](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/real-world-gis-22715766/how-can-you-master-the-gis-job-interview-part-2?u=76281980&t=257)** Showcase that you can work alone and in groups with colleagues.
>
> **[4:22](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/real-world-gis-22715766/how-can-you-master-the-gis-job-interview-part-2?u=76281980&t=262)** Now if you can answer these specifics, you will convince your employer of your worth.
>
> **[4:28](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/real-world-gis-22715766/how-can-you-master-the-gis-job-interview-part-2?u=76281980&t=268)** The other candidates won't stand a chance because of your preparation and execution.
>
> **[4:33](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/real-world-gis-22715766/how-can-you-master-the-gis-job-interview-part-2?u=76281980&t=273)** Now go get that job.
